
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Census Measure - Count - Percentage Of Total]
 AS 
IIF(([Measures].[Census Measure - Count], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent) = 0, 
     null,
     [Measures].[Census Measure - Count]/([Measures].[Census Measure - Count], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent)
    )
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='"#,##0.####', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Census Measures';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - Diagnosis - Start]
 AS IIF ((PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])) = 0  , NULL,
    IIF ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count] = 0, NULL,
            (
            [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count] - 
            (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])
                            )
            )
            / (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])
            )
        )
) 
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - Percent Rank Excluding Null All] as
IIF(isnull((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year]))
    or count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year])) <= 1
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),
				[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year]
			)
		) - 1.0
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Excluding Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - Percent Rank Including Null All] as
IIF((count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year])) - 1.0) <= 1,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, 
			[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year]
		) -1.0
	) / (count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year])) - 1.0)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Including Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[ED Visit - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - ED Visit - Arrival]
 AS IIF ((PARALLELPERIOD([Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[ED Visit - Count])) = 0  , NULL,
    IIF ([Measures].[ED Visit - Count] = 0, NULL,
            (
            [Measures].[ED Visit - Count] - 
            (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[ED Visit - Count])
                            )
            )
            / (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - ED Visit - Arrival].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[ED Visit - Count])
            )
        )
) 
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

     null,

    )
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='"#,##0.####', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

    or count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Lab Order - Count])) <= 1

			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),

	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - Lab Order - Ordered]
 AS IIF ((PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count])) = 0  , NULL,
    IIF ([Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count] = 0, NULL,
            (
            [Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count] - 
            (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count])
                            )
            )
            / (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Lab Order - Ordered].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Lab Order - Encounter - Unique Count])
            )
        )
) 
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Lab Order - Encounter';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Medication Order Quantity - Sum - Percentage Of Total]

     [Measures].[Medication Order Quantity - Sum]/([Measures].[Medication Order Quantity - Sum], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent)
    )

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Surgical Case - Count - Percentile] as
IIF(count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count])) <= 1
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[Surgical Case - Count]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),

			)
		) - 1.0
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Surgical Case';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Surgical Procedure Event - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - Surgery]

                            )
            )

            )
